 The Lucknow bench of the Allahabad High Court has directed the Center, Uttar Pradesh government and the CBI to file a reply to the PIL in which seven districts of the state were investigated for alleged financial irregularities in the Mahatma Gandhi National Rural Employment Guarantee Scheme (MGNREGA)
 The CBI has been requested to order the order
 nyaayamurti pradeep kaant or nyaayamurti devendra kumaar upaadhyaay kii khandpeeth ne yah aadesh ek sthaneey patrkaar kii janhit yachika par diye
 The petition urges the CBI to order an inquiry into alleged financial irregularities in MNREGA in Kushinagar, Gonda, Sonbhadra, Mirzapur, Sant Kabirnagar, Mahoba and Balrampur in the state
 yachi ke vakil gaurav mehrotra ne ‘bhashaa’ ko bataaya ki yachika main kaha gaya he ki chunki yachikakarta ne gonda, mahoba or balrampur main manaregaa main dhaandhlee kii shikaayat kii thi
 In this connection, it was revealed in the State Quality Review Report that similar irregularities have also occurred in Kushinagar, Sonbhadra, Mirzapur and Sant Kabir Nagar
 unhone bataaya ki kendriya graamy vikaas mantri jairam ramesh ne gat 14 navambar ko uttar pradesh sarkaar ko bheje patr main usase is prakaran kii sibiai se jaanch karaane kii sifarish karne kii guzarish kii thi
 There was no action in this direction, so the petitioner moved the court

 Referring to the Indian Air Force air strike on terrorists after the February 14 terror attack in Pulwama, President Ramnath Kovind said that India will use its full strength to protect the sovereignty of the nation
 coimbatore ke hakimpet sthit airforce stesan par ek kaarykram ko sambodhit karte hue raashtrapati ne kaha ki vibhinn deshon ke pariprekshya main antarrashtriya str par jaise-jaise bharat kaa kad badha he thik vaise-vaise uski sashastr sena kii takat or kshamta bhi badi he
 Kovind said that India is determined for peace but if needed we will use our full strength to protect the sovereignty of the nation
 mujhe yakeen he ki sena main hamaare shoorveer purush or bahadur mahila sainik aise samay main apana damakham dikhaaenge
 He said that the armed forces of the country, equipped with brave air warriors, demonstrate this determination to protect the nation
 raashtrapati ne kaha ki hamane unki veerta or peshewar andaaj ko haal main hi dekha he
 This is an example of the way the Indian Air Force carried out attacks targeting terrorist targets
 bhartiya vayusena ne 26 farvari ko air strike kar pakistan main sthit aatankwaadi sanghathan jaish-e-mohammad ke thikaanon ko tabah kar diya tha
 President Kovind attended the President's Colors Award Program at Hakimpet Air Force Station and Sulur's 5 Base Repair Depot where he spoke
 aapako bataa de ki raashtrapati teen divasiy daure par hai
 What is President's Colors is the highest award given by the President to the Air Force contingent or squadron for their unique work and contribution to the service of the country
 ab tak 67 airforce kii uniton or squadran ko ye puraskaar mil chukaa he

 tamaam anushasano main 15,000 se zyada chaatr-chatraayen or 100 se zyada graduate or undergraduate tathaa postagraduate program ke saath galgotiya uniwarsity kaa shiksha ke kshetra main vaishvik santhaan banane kii raah par he
 Dedication to excellence in teaching, research and innovation are the things that make this university a true center of education
 chancelar sunil galgotiya kehete hai ki galgotiya uniwarsity main behtareen se bhi behtareen nikaalane kii kshamta he

 takreeban 15,000 pratibhavan chaatro ke saath galgotiya medhaavi chaatro ko 100' scolership detii he

 galgotiya uniwarsity ke chancelar sunil galgotiyagalgotiya uniwarsity ke chancelar sunil galgotiya kehete hai ki galgotiya uniwarsity main ham sunishchit karte hai ki ham chaatro ko bauddhik, saamaajik or nijee taur par gaharaai se badalane vaala tajurba pradaan karen, jo unhen apni jindagi main naagarikta or netritv ke liye taiyaar kare
 Our emphasis on 360 degree change is because we work as an institution committed to excellence at all levels
 galgotiya uniwarsity ucch shiksha ke liye aane vaale yogya or kshamtawan chaatr-chaatraon ke pansadeeda santhaan ke taur par ubhar rahi he
 We constantly strive to provide world-class facilities and modalities and this has ensured that Galgotia University has become a preferred recruitment ground for blue-chip corporate companies
 hamaare graduate ne vaicharik agua kaa darja hasil kiya he jo nai-nai khoj karke, gyaan ko badhaakar, udhyamshiltaa ko protsaahan dekar, hamaare prakritik paryaavaran ko bachaakar or uski raksha karke tathaa nai technology viksit karke hamaare vaishvik bhavishya kii aguai kar rahe hai
 We believe that in the classroom we begin with the introduction of new ideas, new ways of understanding and new paths of learning and then our students embark on a new journey of intellectual metamorphosis
 saadhaaran shuruyaat karne ke baad sunil galgotiya ne ek lanbaa rasta tay kiya he
 When it comes to giving credit for this success, he says that success is an expression of vision and hard work filled with enthusiasm and enthusiasm
 main apni safalataa kaa shrey ishwar ke aashirwad, apane parivaar or us bahut zyada kadi mehnat ko detaa hum jo maine acchhee talim pradaan karne ke apane lakshya ko saakaar karne ke liye kii he
 It has been a very difficult but at the same time very informative and rewarding journey in many respects
 shiksha harek pragatisheel raashtra kii neenv hoti he
 Where does India stand today? On this question, Galgotia says that education is worship and worship
 iske liye bhi itane hi shuddh prayaas, samarpan or pavitrataa kii jarurat he
 India, like every other developing country, is in the phase of implementing experiments and their results
 bharat sarkaar ko or shiksha kshetra ke nijee sansthaanon ko chahie ki ve duniya bhar main chal rahe bauddhik or technology ke rujhaanon kii jaankaree rakhen or rashtriya tathaa antarrashtriya hakikaton ke sandarbh main apane chaatr samudaay kii psico-somatic profile ko samajhen
 Many changes are needed in the current education scenario of India today
 galgotiya kehete hai ki bharat main ucch shiksha ko behatar banane ke liye centre or rajya sarkaron ne philhal bahut navonmeshi nitiyaan banaai or lagu kii hai
 However, most of the institutes are still running on very old methods of teaching and they do not have the necessary infrastructure
 padhai ke liye shikshan kii kala or shikshashastra main bahut zyada sudhaar kii jarurat he
 Graduates of higher education institutions need to be equipped with analytical and innovative skills to solve problems
 kya bharat ko ucch shiksha main chaatro kaa namakan badhaane kii jarurat he? galgotiya haa main jawaab dete hue kehete hai ki bharat ko jarurat is baat kii he ki vah vishwastareey shiksha sansthaanon ko antarrashtriya str ke paathyakramon ke saath aage badaye
 It needs to get rid of the traditional hurdles because the world today is fast turning into a "human society" due to internet connectivity

 is ap se desh bhar main vibhinn bhashaaon ke madhyam se jan saamaanya ko hindi seekhney main suvidha or saralata hogi tathaa hindi bhashaa ko samajhaana, siikhnaa tathaa kaary karnaa sambhav ho sakegaa
 The comments ullekhneey he ki hindi bhashaa ke deshvyapee prasar or sweekaaryata ko dekhte hue 14 sitambar, 1949 ko ise desh kii rajbhasha kaa darja diya gaya tha
 In commemoration of this day, 14 September is celebrated every year as Hindi Day
